href="/wiki/Club_Deportivo_Guadalajara" class="mw-redirect" title="Club Deportivo Guadalajara">Guadalajara</a> with 11, and <a href="/wiki/Deportivo_Toluca_F.C." title="Deportivo Toluca F.C.">Toluca</a> with 10.<sup id="cite_ref-354" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-354">&#91;354&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Carbajal" title="Antonio Carbajal">Antonio Carbajal</a> was the first player to appear in five World Cups,<sup id="cite_ref-355" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-355">&#91;355&#93;</a></sup> and <a href="/wiki/Hugo_S%C3%A1nchez" title="Hugo S\xc3\xa1nchez">Hugo S\xc3\xa1nchez</a> was named best <a href="/wiki/CONCACAF" title="CONCACAF">CONCACAF</a> player of the 20th century by IFFHS.<sup id="cite_ref-356" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-356">&#91;356&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg/220px-Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg" width="220" height="140" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg/330px-Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/71/Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg/440px-Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1282" data-file-height="814" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Estadio_de_beisbol_en_Monterrey.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Game at the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_de_B%C3%A9isbol_Monterrey" title="Estadio de B\xc3\xa9isbol Monterrey">Estadio de B\xc3\xa9isbol Monterrey</a>. Baseball is most popular in the North (particularly Northwest) and Southeast of Mexico.</div></div></div>\n<p>The Mexican professional baseball league is named the <a href="/wiki/Liga_Mexicana_de_Beisbol" class="mw-redirect" title="Liga Mexicana de Beisbol">Liga Mexicana de Beisbol</a>. While usually not as strong as the United States, the Caribbean countries and Japan, <a href="/wiki/Mexico_national_baseball_team" title="Mexico national baseball team">Mexico</a> has nonetheless achieved several international baseball titles.<sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">&#91;<i><a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed"><span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (March 2011)">citation needed</span></a></i>&#93;</sup> Mexican teams have won the <a href="/wiki/Caribbean_Series" title="Caribbean Series">Caribbean Series</a> nine times. Mexico has had several players signed by Major League teams, the most famous of them being Dodgers pitcher <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Valenzuela" title="Fernando Valenzuela">Fernando Valenzuela</a>.\n</p><p>Mexico City hosted the <a href="/wiki/1968_Summer_Olympics" title="1968 Summer Olympics">XIX Olympic Games</a> in 1968, making it the first Latin American city to do so.<sup id="cite_ref-357" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-357">&#91;357&#93;</a></sup> The country has also hosted the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Cup" title="FIFA World Cup">FIFA World Cup</a> twice, in <a href="/wiki/1970_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1970 FIFA World Cup">1970</a> and <a href="/wiki/1986_FIFA_World_Cup" title="1986 FIFA World Cup">1986</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-358" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-358">&#91;358&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>In 2013, <a href="/wiki/Mexico%27s_basketball_team" class="mw-redirect" title="Mexico&#39;s basketball team">Mexico\'s basketball team</a> won the <a href="/wiki/2013_FIBA_Americas_Championship" title="2013 FIBA Americas Championship">Americas Basketball Championship</a> and qualified for the <a href="/wiki/2014_Basketball_World_Cup" class="mw-redirect" title="2014 Basketball World Cup">2014 Basketball World Cup</a> where it reached the playoffs. Because of these achievements the country earned the hosting rights for the <a href="/wiki/2015_FIBA_Americas_Championship" title="2015 FIBA Americas Championship">2015 FIBA Americas Championship</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-359" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-359">&#91;359&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Bullfighting" title="Bullfighting">Bullfighting</a> is a popular sport in the country, and almost all large cities have bullrings. <a href="/wiki/Plaza_M%C3%A9xico" class="mw-redirect" title="Plaza M\xc3\xa9xico">Plaza M\xc3\xa9xico</a> in Mexico City, is the largest bullring in the world, which seats 55,000 people. Professional wrestling (or <a href="/wiki/Lucha_libre" title="Lucha libre">Lucha libre</a> in Spanish) is a major crowd draw with national promotions such as <a href="/wiki/Lucha_Libre_AAA_World_Wide" class="mw-redirect" title="Lucha Libre AAA World Wide">AAA</a>, <a href="/wiki/Consejo_Mundial_de_Lucha_Libre" title="Consejo Mundial de Lucha Libre">CMLL</a> and others.\n</p>\n<table class="toccolours" style="float:right; margin:0 0 1em 1em; border:1px #ddd solid;">\n<caption>\n</caption>\n<tbody><tr style="text-align:center;">\n<td style="width:130px;"><br />Old <a href="/wiki/Mesoamerican_ballgame" title="Mesoamerican ballgame">Mesoamerican ballgame</a>\n</td>\n<td style="width:100px;"><a href="/wiki/File:232901774_10376f0786.jpg" class="image"><img alt="232901774 10376f0786.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/58/232901774_10376f0786.jpg/165px-232901774_10376f0786.jpg" width="165" height="110" class="thumbborder" class="mw-redirect" title="Charrer\xc3\xada">Charrer\xc3\xada</a>, considered a national sport,<sup id="cite_ref-360" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-360">&#91;360&#93;</a></sup> have its origin in Colonial Mexico.\n</td>\n<td style="width:140px;"><a href="/wiki/File:El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg" class="image"><img alt="El Hijo De Santo vs Blue Demon Jr.jpg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg/87px-El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg" width="87" height="130" class="thumbborder" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg/130px-El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg/174px-El_Hijo_De_Santo_vs_Blue_Demon_Jr.jpg 2x" data-file-width="334" data-file-height="500" /></a><br /><a href="/wiki/Lucha_libre" title="Lucha libre">Mexican wrestling</a>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n<p>Mexico is an international power in <a href="/wiki/Professional_boxing" title="Professional boxing">professional boxing</a> (at the amateur level, <a href="/wiki/Mexico_at_the_Olympics" title="Mexico at the Olympics">several Olympic boxing medals</a> have also been won by Mexico). <a href="/wiki/Vicente_Saldivar" title="Vicente Saldivar">Vicente Saldivar</a>, <a href="/wiki/Rub%C3%A9n_Olivares" title="Rub\xc3\xa9n Olivares">Rub\xc3\xa9n Olivares</a>, <a href="/wiki/Salvador_S%C3%A1nchez" title="Salvador S\xc3\xa1nchez">Salvador S\xc3\xa1nchez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Julio_C%C3%A9sar_Ch%C3%A1vez" title="Julio C\xc3\xa9sar Ch\xc3\xa1vez">Julio C\xc3\xa9sar Ch\xc3\xa1vez</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ricardo_Lopez_Nava" class="mw-redirect" title="Ricardo Lopez Nava">Ricardo Lopez</a> and <a href="/wiki/Erik_Morales" class="mw-redirect" title="Erik Morales">Erik Morales</a> are but a few Mexican fighters who have been ranked among the best of all time.<sup id="cite_ref-361" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-361">&#91;361&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Notable Mexican athletes include golfer <a href="/wiki/Lorena_Ochoa" title="Lorena Ochoa">Lorena Ochoa</a>, who was ranked first in the <a href="/wiki/LPGA" title="LPGA">LPGA</a> world rankings prior to her retirement,<sup id="cite_ref-362" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-362">&#91;362&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ana_Guevara" title="Ana Guevara">Ana Guevara</a>, former world champion of the 400 metres (1,300&#160;ft) and Olympic subchampion in Athens 2004, <a href="/wiki/Fernando_Platas" title="Fernando Platas">Fernando Platas</a>, four-time Olympic medal winning diver, and  taekwondo fighter <a href="/wiki/Mar%C3%ADa_Espinoza" title="Mar\xc3\xada Espinoza">Mar\xc3\xada Espinoza</a>, most decorated Mexican female Olympian.\n</p>\n<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</span></h3>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Coat_of_arms_of_Mexico" title="Coat of arms of Mexico">Coat of arms of Mexico</a></div>\n<p>The current coat of arms of Mexico (<a href="/wiki/Spanish_language" title="Spanish language">Spanish</a>: <i lang="es">Escudo Nacional de M\xc3\xa9xico</i>, literally "national shield of Mexico") has been an important symbol of politics and culture of Mexico for centuries. It depicts a Mexican <a href="/wiki/Golden_eagle" title="Golden eagle">golden eagle</a> perched on a <a href="/wiki/Opuntia" title="Opuntia">prickly pear cactus</a> devouring a <a href="/wiki/Rattlesnake" title="Rattlesnake">rattlesnake</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-Minahan_363-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Minahan-363">&#91;363&#93;</a></sup> The design is rooted in the legend that the <a href="/wiki/Aztec" class="mw-redirect" title="Aztec">Aztec</a> people would know where to build their <a href="/wiki/City" title="City">city</a> once they saw an eagle eating a snake on top of a lake.<sup id="cite_ref-Minahan_363-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Minahan-363">&#91;363&#93;</a></sup> To the people of <a href="/wiki/Tenochtitlan" title="Tenochtitlan">Tenochtitlan</a>, this symbol had strong religious connotations, and to the Europeans, it came to symbolize the triumph of good over evil (with the snake sometimes representative of the serpent in the <a href="/wiki/Garden_of_Eden" title="Garden of Eden">Garden of Eden</a>).\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Health">Health</span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Healthcare_in_Mexico" title="Healthcare in Mexico">Healthcare in Mexico</a></div>\n<p>Since the early 1990s, Mexico entered a transitional stage in the health of its population and some indicators such as mortality patterns are identical to those found in highly developed countries like Germany or Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-364" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-364">&#91;364&#93;</a></sup> Mexico\'s medical infrastructure is highly rated for the most part and is usually excellent in major cities,<sup id="cite_ref-Health_Care_in_Mexico_365-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Health_Care_in_Mexico-365">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-366" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-366">&#91;366&#93;</a></sup> but rural communities still lack equipment for advanced medical procedures, forcing patients in those locations to travel to the closest urban areas to get specialized medical care.<sup id="cite_ref-brit-mex_122-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-brit-mex-122">&#91;122&#93;</a></sup>  <a href="/wiki/Social_determinants_of_health_in_Mexico" title="Social determinants of health in Mexico">Social determinants of health</a> can be used to evaluate the state of health in Mexico.\n</p><p>State-funded institutions such as <a href="/wiki/Mexican_Social_Security_Institute" title="Mexican Social Security Institute">Mexican Social Security Institute</a> (IMSS) and the <a href="/wiki/Institute_for_Social_Security_and_Services_for_State_Workers" title="Institute for Social Security and Services for State Workers">Institute for Social Security and Services for State Workers</a> (ISSSTE) play a major role in health and social security. Private health services are also very important and account for 13% of all medical units in the country.<sup id="cite_ref-367" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-367">&#91;367&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>Medical training is done mostly at public universities with much specializations done in vocational or internship settings. Some public universities in Mexico, such as the <a href="/wiki/University_of_Guadalajara" title="University of Guadalajara">University of Guadalajara</a>, have signed agreements with the U.S. to receive and train American students in Medicine. Health care costs in private institutions and prescription drugs in Mexico are on average lower than that of its North American economic partners.<sup id="cite_ref-Health_Care_in_Mexico_365-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Health_Care_in_Mexico-365">&#91;365&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Education">Education</span></h2>\n<div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Main article: <a href="/wiki/Education_in_Mexico" title="Education in Mexico">Education in Mexico</a></div>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Biblioteca_Central..jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Biblioteca_Central..jpg/220px-Biblioteca_Central..jpg" width="220" height="164" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Biblioteca_Central..jpg/330px-Biblioteca_Central..jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Biblioteca_Central..jpg/440px-Biblioteca_Central..jpg 2x" data-file-width="2557" data-file-height="1910" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Biblioteca_Central..jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div><a href="/wiki/Central_Library_(UNAM)" title="Central Library (UNAM)">Central Library</a> of the <a href="/wiki/National_Autonomous_University_of_Mexico" title="National Autonomous University of Mexico">National Autonomous University of Mexico</a></div></div></div>\n<p>In 2004, the literacy rate was at 97%<sup id="cite_ref-368" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-368">&#91;368&#93;</a></sup> for youth under the age of 14 and 91% for people over 15,<sup id="cite_ref-369" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-369">&#91;369&#93;</a></sup> placing Mexico at the 24th place in the world rank according to <a href="/wiki/UNESCO" title="UNESCO">UNESCO</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-370" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-370">&#91;370&#93;</a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/National_Autonomous_University_of_Mexico" title="National Autonomous University of Mexico">National Autonomous University of Mexico</a> ranks 190th place in the Top 200 World University Ranking published by The Times Higher Education Supplement in 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-371" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-371">&#91;371&#93;</a></sup> Private business schools also stand out in international rankings. <a href="/wiki/IPADE" class="mw-redirect" title="IPADE">IPADE</a> and <a href="/wiki/EGADE" class="mw-redirect" title="EGADE">EGADE</a>, the business schools of <a href="/wiki/Universidad_Panamericana" class="mw-redirect" title="Universidad Panamericana">Universidad Panamericana</a> and of <a href="/wiki/Monterrey_Institute_of_Technology_and_Higher_Education" title="Monterrey Institute of Technology and Higher Education">Monterrey Institute of Technology and Higher Education</a> respectively, were ranked in the top 10 in a survey conducted by <i><a href="/wiki/The_Wall_Street_Journal" title="The Wall Street Journal">The Wall Street Journal</a></i> among recruiters outside the United States.<sup id="cite_ref-372" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-372">&#91;372&#93;</a></sup>\n</p>\n<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">See also</span></h2>\n<div role="navigation" aria-label="Portals" class="noprint portal plainlist tright" style="margin:0.5em 0 0.5em 1em;border:solid #aaa 1px">\n<ul style="display:table;box-sizing:border-box;padding:0.1em;max-width:175px;background:#f9f9f9;font-size:85%;line-height:110%;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold">\n<li style="display:table-row"><span style="display:table-cell;padding:0.2em;vertical-align:middle;text-align:center"><img alt="flag"
